 kuch vidhayak bhi iske virodh menrajya ke shahari vikaas mantri seepi singh or khaadya aapurti mantri sarayu raay sarkaar ke is nirnay se juda raay rakhte hai

 The decision of the government, which is facing opposition from ministers and legislators, is likely to be strongly opposed in rural areas as well
 khaastaur par sharabbandi ke liye muhim chalaa rahi gramin mahilaayein sarkaar ke is kadam se behad naaraaz hai
 What is the decision According to the decision taken in the Cabinet of the Government of Jharkhand, from August 1, the government will sell liquor through Weberz Corporation Limited
 sarkaar kaa maananaa he ki isse sarkaar ke kosh main rajasav mad main 1500 karod aaenge

 kendra sarkaar kii desh ko cashles iconomi kii taraf le jane kii koshishon ke baad digital pement ko i-frod se bachaane ke liye rigerv bank ne sabhi bainkon ko sakht nirdesh jari kiye hai
 The Reserve Bank has ordered all those banks to conduct a special audit from the Indian Computer Emergency Response Team (cert-in) without delay
 iske baad audit kii report ke aadhaar par suraksha ke liye jaruri kadam uthaane ke nirdesh die hai
 Along with this, all banks offering digital payment have been instructed to take all necessary steps to protect their network from phishing attacks at the earliest
 rigerv bank ke mutabikdigital india or cashles iconomiki taraf desh ko le jane ke faisle se badi sankhya main first time yujar in madhyamon kaa istemaal karenge
 This can pose a major threat to banks 'networks and customers' accounts
 lihaaja, rigerv bank ne sabhi bainkon ko agaah kiya he ki vah kisi tarah kii laaparvaahee kii gunjaaish na choden or jaise-jaise dikkatein saamne aati jaaen turant unka nivaaran karne kaa dhaancha taiyaar kar len
 To ensure that all banks and digital payment institutions are properly following these orders, the Reserve Bank has asked them to submit their detailed plans to the Department of Payment and Settlement by 21 December
 isamen unhen apane network kaa audit karaane ke liye auditor kaa naam or samay bhi dena hoga
 According to the Reserve Bank, the trend of online payment and cashless transactions in the country has been increasing rapidly since the closing of the Rs 500 and Rs 1000 currency
 aise main yadi bainkon athwa anya digital pement placeform par sibar atake yaa frod kii ghatnaayen cashles iconomi kii taraf badhate hamaare kadam ko roak sakati hai
 What will happen in this audit? Companies auditing the bank and digital payment platform will closely study their hardware infrastructure, operating system and critical programs
 audit companiyaan yah bhi sunishchit karengi ki bank ke online pement getwe, atm mashin kaa communication placeform, point of cell mashiinon kii security durust or apadated hai ki nahin
 In addition, this audit will also decide whether banks have taken all necessary steps for security or not
 saath hi kisi durghatana yaa sibar atake kii sthiti main unki recovery karnaa or staff ko kisi bhi sthiti se nipatane ke liye training dena bhi shaamil he
 What is cert-in? cert-in is a national nodal agency that takes all precautionary measures to deal with any computer security related incident
 iti act (sanshodhan) 2008 - yah agency sibar security ke liye nimna jaruri kadam uthaane main sakasham hai--sibar atake sambandhit soochnaaon ko ekatrit karnaa, unhen samajhnaa or uskaa prasar karnaa- sibar atake kaa purvanumaan lagaana or alert jari karnaa- sibar atake kii sthiti main apatkaaleen kadam uthaanaa- sibar atake kii sthiti main koordination karnaa- suraksha ke maanakon ko tay karnaa or adwijuri jari karnaa- sibar suraksha se sambandhit die gaye sabhi daayitv ko nibhaana After Bigg Boss 11 winner 'angoori Bhabhi', now actor Arun Govil can also enter politics

 Has been included
